###House Lannister#### 
#####Hear me Roar#####
######################
#Lannisters Ancient History.
#Just updated some things. I got to a chapter in AFoC were Джейме is speaking to his aunt. It's stated that Титос was third-born.
#So rather than mess with his younger brothers Дамон (Джоанна's dad) and Дамион (Lannisport Lannisters). 
#I've added two elder brothers to them all, who died childless. Added random wives for Дамон so Тибольт and Тия are full siblings and one to Тибольт so his five sons are full blooded too.

###A Lannister always pays his debt###
###Ланн the Clever, founder of House Lannister###

				}

		effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { start_date = 8196.6.1 } }
				#set_defacto_liege = ROOT
				set_character_flag = against_king
				set_character_flag = against_loyal_liege

						}
					}
